## Awesome ASCII art for my programs

I often feel like programs should be more fun. Maybe we can make it more alive this way? 

‚ÑπÔ∏è Note: All ASCII arts look best when inserted as comments in most languages. If it looks weird in markdown, look into code and you'll understand

Collected from:
üîó [copypastas](https://www.twitchquotes.com/copypastas/ascii-art)
